General Chiang Kai-shek's Speech on National Salvation Education in Chengdu - Implementation of Education Combining Civil and Military Affairs Is Essential - 99

Chengdu Correspondence, the 17th, 9:00 AM. The third expanded memorial week of General Chiang Kai-shek's visit to Chengdu was held. Attendees included General Chiang Kai-shek

"It all depends on human effort," Luo Fei smiled, trying to cheer up Lu Wen. "Is that right?"

"I hope so."

"Shouldn't you be congratulating me?" Luo Fei changed the subject. "You should be happy."

Lu Wen indeed smiled, and not just a smile, he even jumped with joy.

"Of course, I should congratulate you. I'll buy you a thank-you gift later."

The two of them walked along the left side of the road on the sidewalk. They were heading home. Although they were tired, they felt a lot more energetic. They looked proud, and the sky seemed to deliberately brighten up to illuminate their path ahead.

"I forgot to ask you, when do you officially start working?" Lu Wen suddenly remembered. "When does it start?"

"Tomorrow at nine."

"Tomorrow you'll be a person with a job."

"Our life will be a little more settled."

But Lu Wen thought of something else with ulterior motives. Why did he have to think about this? He felt bad. He felt that his wife's employment was not a success of her skills, but rather similar to the yellow aspect of a prostitute. However, confining his wife at home to be a good wife and mother was not his idea either. He had always advocated that women, like men, should serve society and do things.

When there is no job, you are afraid of not finding one. When you have a job, you think of other side issues. How contradictory!

Luo Fei was also recalling the moment in the manager's house earlier. When she thought about it, she was worried about her future. If the manager continued to be frivolous, how would she deal with it? The continuation of her job also depended on him. As long as he was unhappy for a moment, she could be sacrificed. It seemed that she could not act against his wishes, but if she did, there would be more problems later. After thinking and thinking, she couldn't come up with a safe solution. The final decision was still to act as she had answered Lu Wen: It all depends on human effort. She added an explanation: Stay if it suits, leave if it doesn't.

Lu Wen walked along and bought two packets of peanuts. He kept one for himself and handed the other to his wife, smiling and saying:

"Fei, this is my congratulatory gift to you."

"Too meager. Well, a small gift with great meaning."

Luo Fei also smiled.

The customs clock was pointing to twelve o'clock. Small clerks from companies and banks took buses or trams to go home for lunch, while others went to nearby restaurants to fill their stomachs. Every vehicle was very crowded. "Another one behind!" the ticket seller shouted.

Lu Wen and Luo Fei were also a little hungry and wanted to hurry home to cook. After walking for a while, Lu Wen led his wife onto a bus. After they sat down, he whispered:

"Anyway, we've got a job, let's join the hustle and bustle." Director He, Chairman Liu, Director Kang, Secretary-General Yang, Living Buddha Nuona, and military generals, party and government officials, and representatives from all walks of life, about 1,300 people, were presided over by General Chiang Kai-shek. After performing the rituals, General Chiang Kai-shek gave a speech, the original text of which is as follows:

Chairman Liu, comrades, today our leaders from all walks of life in Chengdu are gathered here again to hold the Memorial Week of the Premier. What I want to say to you is to continue the meaning of what I said in the last Memorial Week, how our leaders from all walks of life should make all those who are taught by us, whether they are children at home, students at school, or subordinates in various institutions and armies, understand the principles of being human in the world and the responsibilities they should bear to the society and the country, and be able to do their best for the society and the country. To achieve this, responsible leaders from all walks of life must be able to lead by example and teach effectively. When it comes to teaching methods, in the past, our ancestors taught people, whether it was family education, school education, or social education, they all emphasized both literary and martial arts, combining civil and military affairs, and cultivating both skills and virtues. They not only wanted to make the educated people understand literary affairs, but also wanted to make them understand martial arts, because if a person does not understand martial arts, he cannot defend himself, protect his neighbors, let alone defend the country and the nation. However, today's education has forgotten this most important principle. Civil and military affairs are completely separated. Literati do not learn martial arts, and warriors do not know literary affairs. It has led to the bad habit of valuing literature and despising martial arts. As a result, each person at most only knows half of the truth. Therefore, there is no complete knowledge, no complete personality, and they cannot fully fulfill their responsibilities as human beings. Therefore, our society and country have been brought to such a state of weakness and danger. Everyone should know that in today's world, all first-class powerful countries have their education that combines civil and military affairs and emphasizes both. It can be said that their education methods are exactly the same as those of our ancestors. For example, the so-called five major powers, Britain, America, France, Italy, and Japan, are all like this. Especially modern emerging countries, such as Germany, Russia, and Turkey, all prioritize martial arts. Not only men have to learn martial arts, but women also have to learn martial arts. Therefore, they can promote the strong and vigorous national spirit, create a magnificent national power, and complete their cause of national revival. From this, it can be seen that if we want to be modern citizens and revive our country and nation from decline and danger, we must correct the bad habit of valuing literature and despising martial arts, restore the ancient education of "combining civil and military affairs," and make all compatriots, regardless of men, women, old or young, have martial arts and be able to defend themselves and the country. Secondly, where should we start learning martial arts? The only important thing is to first forge a strong physique, because if the people do not have a strong physique, they will not have a strong spirit and sufficient strength to fulfill their national responsibilities. In this way, the country cannot be strong and the nation cannot be revived. If we want the country to be strong and the nation to be revived, we must first make the people's physique strong. As for the methods of forging a physique, there are of course many. Now I can put forward a most important principle, which is to fight against the three companions of nature: "sunlight, air, and water." Whether we are educating children at home, educating students at school, or educating soldiers in the army, we must lead by example and make them fight against these three things "sunlight, air, and water" at all times. We must continuously fight against various harsh climates such as severe cold, hot summer, strong winds, heavy rain, frost, and snow to forge our physique. Ordinary people are afraid of heat in hot weather and afraid of cold in winter. They are afraid of being exposed to the hot sun in the hot sun and afraid of getting wet and cold in heavy rain and snow. They dare not go out to work. This is simply being conquered by nature. We must overcome nature. The colder and hotter it is, the more we must go out to work. The stronger the wind and snow, the more excited and hardworking we must be. If we cannot control these three things, sunlight, air, and water, we will be controlled by them. This kind of person will not have any achievements. All ambitious people, no matter how cold or hot the weather is, how strong the sunlight is, or how heavy the rain and snow are, always fight against them. In this way, they will definitely be able to overcome them, forge a physique of bronze muscles and iron bones, and be able to stand tall and achieve success. However, now not only general literary schools do not pay attention to this important method of forging the body, but even the army, which is generally regarded as specializing in martial arts, has not really done this. Since everyone does not know how to use this method to forge the body, the physique and spirit of our general people are weakening day by day. No wonder the country and nation are also declining day by day. Therefore, from now on, whether they are leaders in literature or martial arts, or in agriculture, industry, commerce, and academia, they must know that the first priority of teaching people is to forge their physique, so that it becomes stronger and stronger day by day. This is more important than any other thing or any other knowledge. Of course, if we want to make the general people physically strong, we must first make them quit all the bad habits that harm the body, such as opium and gambling. However, we must lead by example and explain to them that in order to survive and thrive in the world, one must first seek to be healthy, and make them fight against nature such as sunlight and water. Of course, they will not go back to smoking or gambling. We must always start teaching people with this kind of forging of the physique, and then we can teach other knowledge and morality. We must also have a strong physique in order to exert all our intelligence and talents to take on major tasks for the society and the country. The above is about forging a physique with the best method. Martial arts can not only forge a physique, but it is also an indispensable skill for protecting the country and defending the people. Now not only literati do not understand martial arts, but to be honest, even general warriors do not understand martial arts. Although they wear military hats and military uniforms, and formally look like soldiers, they not only do not understand literary affairs, but they do not even understand the principles of martial arts. In the eyes of foreigners, they are all nondescript, neither literary nor military, and half-dead people. What is "martial arts" that I am talking about? It not only refers to techniques such as shooting guns and cannons, but the most important thing is the spirit of applying martial arts, that is, the martial virtues of wisdom, faith, benevolence, courage, and strictness, as the ancients called them. We, as warriors, must be equipped with "resourcefulness," "trustworthiness," "benevolence," "courage," and "strictness" in order to be considered true warriors. If we only know a little bit of techniques such as shooting guns and cannons, but do not have martial virtues, this is only barbarism and cannot be considered understanding martial arts. This kind of person is a fake warrior who harms the country and the people. We wear military hats, military uniforms, and are warriors. It is absolutely not enough to just know how to use martial arts and be able to fight. We must have martial virtues and fulfill our duty to protect the country and defend the people. Only in this way can we become true warriors and true complete people. The general people will love and support this kind of warrior, and will never have any aversion to them. Why do the general people despise our soldiers now? It is because the general soldiers, although they wear military hats and military uniforms, do not know martial virtues and do not know how to fulfill the responsibilities of soldiers for the country and the people. They are completely fake warriors, not true warriors. Why does our country lack true warriors so much? It is because the people who were responsible for military education in the past did not understand the principles of being warriors, so they could not teach the general students or subordinates well. From the time general students enter military academies to the time they graduate, and from the time general troops enter the army for training to the time they are able to fight, they are only taught a little bit of martial arts, and martial virtues are not taught at the same time, and the entire martial arts are not passed on to them. Therefore, they cannot promote the true spirit of soldiers and create the true strength of soldiers to protect the country and defend the people, which has led the country to such a critical state of survival. Therefore, if we want to be upright and honorable soldiers in the universe, we must first have martial virtues. Therefore, I hope that leaders from all walks of life, whether teaching children, teaching students, or teaching subordinates, should pay attention to this point. If we want to make them modern citizens, they must have martial arts. If we want to have martial arts, we must first have martial virtues. If everyone can promote martial virtues and increase martial arts, then there is no reason why the country and nation cannot turn from weak to strong and from danger to safety. Secondly, when it comes to the main content of education, the ancients educated students in the so-called six arts of ritual, music, archery, charioteering, writing, and mathematics. From this, it can be seen that the education of our ancient China was originally a combination of civil and military affairs and a cultivation of both skills and virtues. Now, most people think that literary schools only teach literary affairs and do not teach martial arts, which is completely wrong. In the future, school education should still be based on the ancient spirit of "combining civil and military affairs" and the principle of "cultivating the six arts," but the content of education should be enriched and advanced. Because the six arts that the ancients spoke of are actually the basic qualities and skills that modern citizens must possess. At the beginning of students and soldiers entering school or joining the army, these subjects should be used to teach them. These subjects can be learned by anyone. The so-called "ritual" is to summarize all reasonable attitudes and rules for conducting oneself and dealing with others. It does not specifically refer to bowing and raising hands in a narrow sense. These ordinary rituals can only be regarded as small rituals. What we mean is that whether we are eating, living, speaking, or acting, we must have rules and order at all times. Our lives for twenty-four hours a day are all within the bounds of ritual. If we do not observe ritual for a moment, families, schools, armies, and even the society and the country will be in chaos. Therefore, the ancients said, "Ritual is the governance of things," and also said, "Ritual is the foundation." From this, it can be seen the importance of ritual. Now, most people do not understand this important principle and think that preaching ritual education is a legacy of the feudal system and is not suitable for modern times. They do not know that ritual is the fundamental condition for establishing oneself and dealing with the world. Whether in ancient or modern times, at home or abroad, it cannot be separated for a moment. If school teachers or army officers do not educate their students or subordinates with ritual, they will become rude and lawless people. Not only will they themselves not be able to become talented and be good people, but the society and the country will also suffer their harm. Everyone should know that the standard of civilization of a person to a country is how well their people follow ritual and how well they follow the law. Now, foreigners scold us for not being a modern country, which means that our general people do not value ritual, do not abide by the law, have no order, and have no organization. In fact, as long as those of us who are responsible for education can lead by example and pay attention to education, ritual is something that people can know and that everyone can easily practice. For example, when students first enter school, they are taught to respect teachers and love classmates in school, to respect parents and love siblings at home, and to respect elders and love compatriots in society, wherever they go, to have etiquette and observe order. There is nothing they do not understand in these things, and there is nothing they cannot do when they understand them. Whether we are teaching students or teaching soldiers, we must first teach them the most important and easy-to-know and easy-to-practice principles. The "ritual" we are talking about now is the most important and easy-to-know and easy-to-practice principle. If everyone can use ritual as a teaching method, they can make all those who are taught successful and honorable modern citizens. The so-called "music" is music. Good music can cultivate temperament, invigorate the spirit, comfort labor, and harmonize the mind, making people's lives smooth and their interests beautiful, and invisibly cultivating personal personality and pure social customs. Its importance is not only related to the cultivation of personal morality, but also affects the rise and fall of society and the country. If a person does not have musical cultivation, their life is often easily dry and extreme, and instability, chaos, or even chaos can arise from this. Conversely, if we have musical cultivation, we can be comforted when we are bored, and we can turn to peace and solemnity when we are noisy and disturbed. Sad people can be turned into happy people, violent people can be turned into gentle people, and depressed people can be suddenly excited. From this, it can be seen that the function of music is very important. If a person does not understand music, they will not know the occasion for joy, anger, sorrow, and happiness, and cannot achieve a perfect life. If a school, army, or society and country does not have music, it cannot be a perfect school, army, or society and country. Especially for the army, music is the most important. We usually need to harmonize the military's mind, align the steps, unite the spirit, and in wartime, we need to comfort the tired, inspire morale, and boost the military's prestige, all of which depend on military music. When I was suppressing bandits in Jiangxi, I compiled a song for suppressing bandits, and this song had a great effect. Therefore, you general senior generals must pay special attention to military music and military songs. Roughly speaking, the first element of music is to require harmony. The pitch, intensity, length, and shortness of the rhythm must be neat and in accordance with the rhythm and beat to play the role of music. Today, the tone of everyone's party song is not harmonious. Everyone is a leader from all walks of life, and they still sing so unevenly, which is really something that should not happen. Everyone should pay attention to improving in the future, and they must teach their students and subordinates to understand music, so that they can become all-rounders in the future. We humans all have musical talent. Even a three-year-old child, if we teach them to sing, they will sing. So anyone can do it. Now our society does not pay much attention to music. Except for music majors in schools, general teachers and students do not pay attention to music. Now that we understand that music has such a significant relationship with people's hearts and customs and with society and the country, we must vigorously promote it in the future. The so-called "archery" in ancient times was archery, which was a martial art that everyone had to learn. And they often held grand archery ceremonies. When the archery ceremony was held, it was a very glorious thing for the person who could hit the target. The ancients said, "A gentleman has nothing to compete for, but archery. He yields and ascends, and drinks when he descends. His competition is gentlemanly." From this, it can be seen that the ancients attached great importance to archery, and the essence of archery can also be seen from this. The so-called archery refers to archery. Now that guns and cannons have been invented, the word archery also refers to shooting. The cultivation of this skill is very important for the people's morality, people's wisdom, and the rise and fall of society and the country. Now there is shooting everywhere abroad. People from families, schools, armies, and various institutions participate in this organization. Both men and women can shoot. Looking back at our general people, not only can they not shoot, but they have never even seen it. In today's world, the people are so lacking in this important cultivation. How can they be modern citizens and not be invaded and oppressed by others? Therefore, everyone must know the importance of shooting and vigorously promote it, so that shooting associations can be organized everywhere, and the general people can master the art of shooting to protect the country and defend the people. The so-called "charioteering" is about riding horses and driving carriages. Now many people think that this is a very lowly thing. They do not know that this is also a skill that the ancients valued very much. For example, Confucius' students often held whips and drove carriages for the elders. In ancient China, many children drove carriages for their parents and teachers. Both literati and warriors could ride horses and practice martial arts. Now everyone does not do these things, and they do not even mention them. Not only do they not drive carriages for their parents and elders, but many children still ask their parents and brothers to carry their luggage when they go out to study. Are these people still considered polite? Now that airplanes and cars have been invented, driving airplanes and cars is also called charioteering. Although the tools and technologies have changed, the meaning and importance of "charioteering" remain the same. Everyone should know that "charioteering" is the principle of driving and controlling things. In a broad sense, it can include all of human intelligence. In a narrow sense, it specifically refers to the driving of moving tools, which is also a necessary skill for modern citizens, especially soldiers. Therefore, everyone should not think that "charioteering" is a lowly thing, but should pay attention to using it to educate general students and subordinates. In addition, the so-called "writing" and "mathematics," "writing" refers to writing and literature, and "mathematics" refers to mathematics, statistics, measurement, and various other skills related to mathematics. This is what general people know they should pay attention to. I do not need to talk much about it now. In short, the six arts of ritual, music, archery, charioteering, writing, and mathematics are the important content of education that combines civil and military affairs, and they are also the indispensable skills of a modern country. All those who are responsible for teaching students and subordinates, if they do not teach people with these six arts, so that the educated people become talents, they cannot be considered complete teachers. To be a model teacher, they must have considerable cultivation in all six arts, and they must teach the principles of the six arts to the general educated people at the same time. They must teach the corresponding skills according to the degree of the educated people and the principle of emphasizing all six arts. We must all understand ritual and music, practice archery and charioteering, and master writing and mathematics. We should not regard this as a specialized academic skill. We must know that the six arts are something that everyone can know and everyone should learn. In the future, if we want to make the general students and subordinates become sound talents and build a modern country, we must implement education that combines civil and military affairs and cultivates both skills and virtues. Today, all the comrades here have the responsibility of teaching people. Therefore, today I specially tell you the principles of teaching people. From now on, everyone should know that if we want to be able to teach the general students and subordinates, and even the general people, to become talents, first, we must make them fight against nature to forge their physique; second, we must teach them the martial virtues of wisdom, faith, benevolence, courage, and strictness; and third, all education must take the six arts of ritual, music, archery, charioteering, writing, and mathematics as its main content. The fundamental spirit of the New Life Movement that I advocate is propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame. Propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame can be connected with wisdom, faith, benevolence, courage, and strictness, which is the fundamental spirit of the six arts. Therefore, if we want to implement education that combines civil and military affairs, the most practical point is to strive to promote the New Life Movement. Today, I take this opportunity to tell everyone the methods of teaching people. If everyone can follow this meaning and work tirelessly, not only will education in Sichuan achieve twice the result with half the effort, and the social atmosphere in Sichuan can be thriving, but also the future of the entire country and nation will be infinitely bright." (Central News Agency, June 20)

Smuggled Soil Dealer Sent to Province for Investigation 101

Jiang Akang, a soil smuggler from Yexie, was on his way back to Ye last month on a Shanghai-bound boat carrying soil when he was spotted by officers from the Yexie Waterborne Provincial Public Security Team, who found his behavior suspicious. Several hundred taels of smuggled soil were found. When questioned, he confessed that he had pooled money with several people to buy and bring back the soil. The case was not fully investigated, but when provincial investigators found out, they reported it to the Provincial Opium Prohibition Committee for review. The Department of Civil Affairs ordered the county to arrest him. He was arrested in Ye yesterday and taken to Songjiang for interrogation. After interrogation, he confessed to the involvement of several people. In addition to continuing to detain them, Jiang Akang was first escorted to the Provincial Garrison Headquarters for investigation by several security team officers.

Wuxi, Wanyuan Money Shop Suddenly Closes 102

The Wanyuan Money Shop, located south of the Shengxiang Bridge in the city, was established by Chen Yitang as his sole proprietorship and has been in business for more than ten years. Its business scope includes small loans, public bond treasury bills, purchase of unpaid yarn coupons from various places, and sales of various prize-winning securities. Its business was considered to be quite developed. In recent years, Chen suffered repeated failures due to speculative business operations and was also affected by the market downturn, resulting in internal emptiness and poor turnover. It suddenly closed yesterday and hired lawyer Qu Zhiyong to clear up the accounts. All creditors are required to register at the office within fourteen days. Chen Yitang himself has temporarily sought refuge in Shanghai to avoid disputes.

Changshu: Exhumation and Bone Examination in Meili Homicide Case 105

Qin Mingyuan, a local vendor from Meili Township in this county, died suddenly after being searched by Liu Chunnan and other anti-opium association investigators. He died within two hours of being detained. The county autopsy determined that he had committed suicide by poisoning to escape punishment. However, Qin's relatives, including his wife Gui and sister Wu Qin, claimed that the deceased had no opportunity to take poison and accused the investigators of extortion and fatal assault. They requested a second autopsy. The Jiangsu High Court dispatched coroner Xuan Fang to Changshu, and the exhumation took place on the 21st at Zhua Pa Wan outside the North Gate. More than ten thousand men and women attended as spectators. County Magistrate Zhai Huan also personally attended the site to supervise the examination. The examination began at 2:00 PM that day. However, due to the decomposition of the body, it was impossible to determine whether he had taken poison or suffered injuries. It was decided to perform a bone examination. At that moment, the deceased's sister, Wu Qin, seeing the dark face and decaying flesh of the deceased, fainted and collapsed, losing all pulse. It nearly resulted in another fatality. Wu Qin pleaded with the County Magistrate to send her to a certain hospital for treatment. After two injections of cardiac stimulant, she gradually recovered. She then cried loudly. As the bone steaming could not be completed in a short time, it was postponed to the morning of the second day. The truth may be revealed by the evening.

Hangzhou: Robbery-Murderer Executed by Firing Squad 106

Jin Rentu, a farmer from Shicang, Linhai County, possessed some property, which made him a target for bandits. Huang Shoutao and others, including "Lai Toad" Little He, armed with guns, raided his home, stealing property and fatally shooting Jin Rentu. Subsequently, military police captured two bandits, Song and He, and executed them by firing squad. Huang was also later apprehended and sentenced to death. He appealed to the provincial court, but the original sentence was upheld. He then appealed to the Supreme Court, which remanded the case for retrial. The death sentence was again imposed. Yesterday morning at 8:00 AM, he was escorted outside Qingtai Gate and executed by firing squad.

Due to continuous heavy rains and the downstream flow of mountain waters from the upper reaches of the Qiantang River, the submerged dams in the areas of Babao and Tasha Dam have collapsed along with the silt outside the dikes due to the impact of huge waves. The situation is quite severe and critical. After receiving a report from the Water Conservancy Bureau, the Fourth Office (of the provincial government) immediately dispatched Jiang Min, the responsible section member, by car to investigate and sent workers to rush to repair the water barriers for prevention and rescue.

Tobacco and Alcohol Tax Conference: General Meeting Held Yesterday, Approving Various Proposals; Strictly Enforcing Rewards and Punishments; Requesting the Ministry of Finance to Improve Tobacco Production; Closing Ceremony Tomorrow, Minister Kong Will Give Another Speech 108

The Xin Sheng News Agency reports that the Ministry of Finance's Taxation Department convened the directors of the provincial stamp, tobacco, and alcohol tax bureaus in Shanghai to hold a tobacco and alcohol tax conference. A discussion meeting was held yesterday morning, and the proposals were passed. Today is Sunday, a day of rest. The closing ceremony will be held tomorrow morning. Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi will attend the meeting and give a speech. The details are recorded as follows:

Yesterday's General Meeting

The general meeting was held in the Junpu Bureau conference room on the fifth floor of the Jianghai Customs House yesterday morning at 9:00 AM. The directors of the provincial bureaus, Zhao Jinqing, Jing Xuxin, Wang Guanghui, Jing Youyan, Qu Dacheng, Yang Duo, Fu Zhengshun, Huang Zupei, Sheng Shengyi, Xue Futian, Tang Yan, and Ding Chungao, as well as Taxation Department Director Wu Qiding, Secretary Dong Zhongding, Zhou Jiechun, Inspectors Tang Shi, Section Chiefs Fang Yunxian, Jiang Yongyi, Hong Yi, Chen Jun, and others, were present. Director Wu presided over the meeting. First, Zhao Jinqing, chairman of the first group that reviewed the proposals, and Ding Chungao, chairman of the second group, reported on the review process. Then, they discussed the proposals separately and adjourned at 1:30 PM.

Resolutions Passed

The resolutions of the General Meeting for the Tobacco and Alcohol Tax Conference are as follows: (1) To strictly determine quotas and vigorously implement performance assessments. (2) To implement both rewards and punishments to rectify tax collection. The above two proposals were discussed together and resolved to pass in accordance with the original proposals. However, the revision of the budget range was changed to be based on the actual collection of each provincial branch bureau in the past three years as the warp, and the recent local production and sales situation and the current collection system as the weft. (3) To implement a contracting system for tobacco and alcohol tax to ensure tax revenue. (4) To fix quotas and restrict collection and delivery with reference to the election committee method to increase tax revenue. The above two proposals were discussed together and resolved to be reserved. (4) The quota of tobacco and alcohol tax in Shandong Province should be allocated according to peak and off-peak months. (5) To set up bureaus by region to facilitate organization. (6) Starting from the 22nd year (of the Republic), the local tobacco tax of Deng County, Xichuan, and other counties should still be collected by the Henan Bureau to clarify jurisdiction and facilitate organization. For the above three proposals, it was resolved that the original proposing provinces should submit special requests for approval. (7) To request that the provincial bureaus prepare tables of the quotas and actual deliveries of each sub-bureau and request the supervisors and staff to submit them in advance. It was resolved to pass in accordance with the original proposal. (8) Which types of alcohol can be changed to a single collection method? It was resolved to pass in principle. Trial implementation will begin in Jiangsu (Taixing, Taixian, Suzhou Hengjing, etc.) for local brews, Hubei (Hanfen), and Zhejiang (Shaojiu). The department will formulate a method and implement it on a regular basis. (9) The tobacco and alcohol tax and fees in Shandong Province should be collected under the same name. (10) To unify tobacco and alcohol prices to maintain commerce and increase tax revenue. (11) To formulate measures for organizing the collection of tobacco and alcohol tax to increase tax revenue. For the above three proposals, it was resolved that the original proposing provinces should submit special requests for approval. (12) To hold a tobacco and alcohol merchant registration in Anhui Province. It was resolved that the regulations on the fixed tax for local alcohol in the Tobacco and Alcohol Merchant Regulations already have provisions. The provincial bureaus can follow the regulations to implement them properly. There is no need to set up a separate organization. (13) To levy taxes separately on duty-paid tobacco leaves that are made into tobacco shreds for non-cigarette use. (14) To change the special tobacco leaf tax to a tax on tobacco shreds. For the above two proposals, it was resolved that the Taxation Department would send them to the provincial bureaus for review. (15) To propose a new tax rate for local tobacco leaves in Anhui Province. It was resolved that the original proposing province should submit a special request for approval. (16) The fixed tax payment and zero-catty duty-paid certificates for local tobacco will be implemented within the next year. (17) Local tobacco should be changed to a fixed tax certificate to facilitate verification. For the above two proposals, it was resolved that the Taxation Department would send the original proposals to the provincial bureaus for review before implementing them. (18) To request a redesign of the duty-paid certificate. It was resolved to pass in principle. The Taxation Department is requested to consider modifications. (19) To prohibit alcohol from being used as a beverage to protect the livelihoods of brewing households. It was resolved to pass in accordance with the original proposal. The Ministry will submit it to the Executive Yuan and hand it over to the competent authorities for review of the measures. (20) To increase the expenses of each sub-bureau. (21) To increase the expenses of each tobacco and alcohol sub-bureau in each district, verify and fill in the licenses to facilitate progress. The above two proposals were discussed together and resolved to provide reasons in principle, but since the national treasury is currently stretched, it should be postponed for further discussion. (22) For the excess amount of tobacco and alcohol tax collected by each sub-bureau, in addition to the 16% commission expense that should be paid, an incremental commission will be used to encourage it. (23) To request the department to stipulate an annual collection bonus method for branch bureau chiefs of tobacco and alcohol inspection and local tobacco special tax to encourage it. The above two proposals were discussed together and resolved to take the provincial bureau's total budget as the standard for awarding bonuses for exceeding the quota. Since the expenses of the branch bureau are already difficult, in order to ensure that the provincial bureaus seriously reorganize, at the end of each year, if the amount of tax collected and delivered by the provincial bureau exceeds the quota set by the Ministry, in addition to the expenses being paid, it is proposed that the Ministry approve the extraction of 20% of the surplus as a bonus to be allocated by the competent provincial bureau for encouragement. (24) To specifically set up inspectors to strictly enforce the pasting of alcohol duty-paid stamps and local tobacco print certificates and prevent the mutual circulation of various branch bureaus. It was resolved that this case is an essential plan at present and can be handled according to the original proposal. (25) To seriously investigate and handle control cases. It was resolved that control cases are related to the rights of merchants and the quality of tax administration. It should be thoroughly investigated. Moreover, in recent years, merchants' control cases have often been submitted to the Control Yuan and the Executive Yuan. It should be seriously investigated so that the Ministry can truthfully reply. This case can be handled according to the original proposal. However, the control procedure should be handled in accordance with the methods promulgated by the Xingying (Northwest Suppression Headquarters). (26) To request all provinces to assist in anti-smuggling. It was resolved that the tobacco and alcohol tax bureaus of each province belong to the national tax authorities and originally have no distinction between each other. They should cooperate fully and assist in contact at any time to connect and prevent evasion. It is proposed that the Ministry of Finance issue an order to all bureaus to investigate and handle it. (27) To request the Ministry to consult the provincial governments of each province to include the officials of the county magistrates who assist the tax authorities in the county magistrate's performance appraisal. (28) To clearly stipulate the reward methods for local officials who have effectively assisted in the collection of tobacco and alcohol taxes and the penalty regulations for tax evasion and promulgate them as soon as possible. The above two proposals were discussed together and resolved to include the county magistrate's assistance in the performance appraisal and to clearly stipulate the reward methods. It is proposed that the Ministry of Finance consult with the Ministry of Interior to handle it. (29) To request the training of tax police to eliminate long-standing malpractices and benefit inspection and collection. It was resolved that the patrol situation varies from province to province. The Taxation Department is planning a whole anti-smuggling method and plans to compile a unified tax police. The case of the Hubei Bureau's plan to compile tax police can be submitted to the Ministry for approval by the Hubei Bureau. (30) To strictly implement spot checks and re-examinations of tobacco and alcohol license taxes in accordance with regulations to re-emphasize tax revenue. It was resolved that the spot checks and re-examinations of license taxes by the provincial tobacco bureaus are the regulations of the Provisional Regulations and Implementation Rules for Tobacco and Alcohol Business License Taxes. It should be handled in accordance with the regulations. However, it should be requested that the Ministry first consult with the provincial governments of each province to order the finance departments to send the register of license taxes collected by each county to the Ministry so that it can order the bureaus to conduct spot checks. For the re-examination section, it can be requested that the Ministry of Finance consult with the provincial governments to order the departments to handle it in accordance with the regulations. (31) To request to modify the penalty rules for fixed local alcohol tax. It was resolved that the original proposal's first, second, fourth, and fifth four items should be submitted to the Ministry of Finance for consideration and adoption when revising the regulations. The third item, if the merchant submits an inconsistent transportation license, it should be investigated and dealt with in accordance with the regulations if it is intentional. If it is an unintentional mistake, it can be exempted from discussion. The regulations in the original regulations on penalty regulations that include inconsistent cargo certificates or transportation licenses and re-transportation certificate are broad and difficult to cancel. The sixth item, the method of supplementing tax and punishing tobacco and alcohol that are smuggled into other provinces, Article 29 of the Jiangsu Alcohol Fixed Tax Implementation Rules is very clear. Each province can stipulate it in the detailed rules of each province. For those who have evaded production tax and those who have evaded sales tax, they should be supplemented separately. However, the penalty can only be imposed concurrently and cannot be imposed separately. The scope of the seventh item of the original proposal seems too broad. If each province encounters tax evasion cases that are not stipulated in the regulations, it may propose methods for handling special cases and report them to the Ministry for approval and the Ministry will issue an order to the provincial bureaus to handle them with reference to them. (32) To change the fine rules to benefit tax revenue. It was resolved that Article 37 of the Local Alcohol Fixed Tax Inspection Regulations stipulates that the confiscated and priced items will be released from the treasury, half of which will be divided into ten shares, and the informant will receive four shares. All fines will be divided into ten shares, and the informant will receive four shares, which is better for rewarding. Shandong Province and other provinces that have not handled fixed tax can handle it with reference to it. It is proposed that the Ministry of Finance issue an order to comply. (34) To request the Ministry to dispatch agricultural technology experts to the tobacco-producing areas to seek all improvements. It was resolved to suggest that the Ministry of Finance handle it appropriately. (35) To form an organization jointly by officials and merchants to lend money to rural areas, improve tobacco seeds, and lend money to brewers and tobacco merchants to advance the purchase of brewing materials and tobacco leaves to benefit production. It was resolved to suggest that the Ministry of Finance hand it over to the provincial bureaus to draft opinions and report for review.

Opening Ceremony Tomorrow Morning

After the proposals submitted by the Taxation Department and the provincial bureau chiefs are passed by yesterday's general meeting, they will be implemented separately. Today is Sunday, a day of rest. Wu Tingsheng and other members of the Cigarette Anti-Smuggling Association are scheduled to jointly host a banquet for the provincial bureau chiefs at 12:00 noon today. The closing ceremony will be held at the Junpu Bureau conference room on the fifth floor of the Jianghai Customs House at 9:00 AM tomorrow morning. Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi will attend the meeting and give a speech. After the closing ceremony, the provincial bureau chiefs will return to their respective posts.

Ministry of Finance Issues Order Promulgating Measures for Punishing Secret Transportation of Silver 115

Refer to the Crime of Endangering the Republic of China's Rule of Law; Yesterday's Instruction, Today's Silver and Money Industries to Comply

The Industry News Agency reports that the Ministry of Finance, in order to address the impact of the private transportation of silver out of the country on domestic finance, has repeatedly and strictly prohibited it in order to stabilize the market. However, a few unscrupulous merchants still secretly plan to smuggle it out. In order to completely eliminate this and maintain financial flow, the Ministry of Finance has specially promulgated the measures for punishing the secret transportation of silver and ordered the provincial and municipal governments and the chambers of commerce and silver and money industries to comply with them. Yesterday, it was learned from the silver and money industries that the instruction was received yesterday. The order stated that the Central Political Conference has decided to hand over the measures for punishing the secret transportation of silver to the Executive Yuan for promulgation. All offenders who privately transport silver coins or silver out of the country or go to places where the silver standard currency is not used will be punished in accordance with the Emergency Crime Control Law of Endangering the Republic of China, with imprisonment of not less than five years and not more than ten years for minor offenses, and life imprisonment or death penalty for serious offenses, etc. This Ministry has submitted a report to the National Government for promulgation and record. It is appropriate to record the case and order immediate compliance and transfer it to the subordinates for compliance. It is heard that after receiving the order, the silver and money industries have notified their members to comply with it.

City Chamber of Commerce Today's Representatives' Assembly Discusses Important Cases Including: 116

Establishing an Industrial and Commercial Revitalization Committee to Study Plans, and Controlling Import Trade and Managing International Exchange Rates

The Shanghai City Chamber of Commerce is scheduled to hold this session's Member Representatives' Assembly today (the 23rd) to discuss important proposals. The details are as follows:

Assembly Staff (1) Presidium: Yu Zuoting, Xu Jiyin, Jin Run, Ke Wuchen; (2) Secretary: Yan Esheng; (3) Master of Ceremonies: Zhu Boggang; (4) Disciplinarian: Luo Qinghua, Wu Shaoquan, Zheng Chengqing, Pan Changsheng, Zheng Zenan; (5) Recorder: Wu Jichun, Zhi Zhong; (6) Reception: Sun Mingqi, Hu Weijian, Yuan Hongjun, Dong Wenzhong, Qian Xingzhong, Zhang Nanyin; (7) Signature: Zhang Yukun, He Tai, Tao Zhen, Li Ruzhang, Xue Jianxin, Ren Shoupeng; (8) Affairs: Liu Zhu, Chen Runyi, Huang Rongshi; (9) Verification: The Chamber of Commerce Boy Scout Group.

Rules of Procedure The meeting room is equipped with an amplified phonograph from the China Wireless Electric Research Society, providing very clear sound transmission. The rules of procedure are as follows: (1) Please stand when speaking; (2) Please report your seat number before speaking; (3) Do not speak simultaneously; (4) Do not speak more than twice on one proposal; (5) Each speech should not exceed five minutes. Extension of time must be requested in advance from the chairman; (6) Please be concise and clear when speaking; (7) Please do not applaud when others are speaking; (8) Please do not speak after the chairman declares the discussion of a case closed; (9) Please do not talk during the meeting to avoid hindering hearing; (10) If you need to leave early, please request permission from the chairman in advance.

Important Proposals This session of the Representatives' Assembly will discuss 16 important proposals from various industries. The most important are the proposal by consultant Wang Yansong to establish an Industrial and Commercial Revitalization Committee to investigate the actual situation of industry and commerce, study revitalization plans, and the proposal by supervisor Luo Qinghua to petition the government to control import trade and manage international exchange rates to prevent import surpluses and safeguard the national foundation. These will be the focus of the assembly's discussions. The original text of the two proposals is recorded below: (1) Mr. Wang Yansong's proposal states: "Since the outflow of silver and the contraction of currency, credit has declined daily, and all industries have suffered. The financial sector lacks the means to circulate funds, and industry and commerce are at a loss. Shanghai, located in the economic and industrial center of the country, is more severely affected than other places. In the past six months, dangerous situations have occurred frequently, and bankruptcies have followed one after another. The perilous situation cannot be ignored. In terms of the current situation in the financial sector, what was once called a shortage of chips has now become a phenomenon of credit disappearance. What was once difficult to circulate and transfer has now become a fact of liquidation and bankruptcy. Although the government has allocated 2.5 million yuan in financial bonds to help overcome the current difficulties, temporary relief cannot compensate for the future circulation of funds in the banking industry. The effect of the allocation is only enough to prolong life. As for the current situation in industry and commerce, the unemployed masses are everywhere. Everything seen and heard, and reported in newspapers, is filled with panic about the severity of the situation, and there is a desire for effective relief from the government. The whole country is in a state of panic and doesn't know what to do. However, after investigating the truth, the extent of the industrial and commercial decline and the crux of the problem have never been thoroughly investigated or analyzed in detail for reference. Other groups are not to blame, but even the industry and commerce themselves, who are suffering, can only sit and wait for death while shouting and clamoring. Speaking of decline in this way is no different from the clamor of the blind. Speaking of revitalization in this way is no different from climbing a tree to catch a fish. It is impossible to prescribe the right medicine to revive and save the situation. Shanghai is the essence of the country's industry and commerce, and this Chamber of Commerce is the highest representative body of Shanghai's industry and commerce. It should have a detailed and clear path for the current decline of various industries. I dare not presume to be foolish and propose the establishment of an Industrial and Commercial Revitalization Committee, inviting economic experts from all parties and extending invitations to leaders of industrial and commercial enterprises to gather together and jointly devise remedies. The result will be to provide guidance for various industries to respond and to provide the government with corresponding choices. I respectfully request that representatives from various industries carefully consider and then decide on the principle of establishing the committee and submit it to the executive committee for prompt implementation to witness its success. Industry and commerce will be fortunate, and the country will be fortunate. Is this appropriate? I respectfully await your decision." (2) Mr. Luo Qinghua's proposal states: "I have investigated that since the records of foreign trade in our country, there has been an import surplus every year, and the number is often between 200 and 300 million customs taels. In the past, we relied on remittances from overseas Chinese, foreign investment, and other intangible income to offset the deficit and make up for the temporary shortage. However, since the wave of the world economic panic in 1929 began to counterattack the globe, all industrialized countries have fallen into the heavy group of overproduction and increasing unemployment. As a result, 'economic nationalism' prevailed internationally for a time. In order to maintain their own domestic markets, countries have built high tariff barriers to restrict the import of foreign goods. In order to expand overseas markets, they have also used monetary policies to implement foreign dumping, scheming against each other and competing for consumer markets. Our country, with its underdeveloped industry and backward production, is not self-sufficient and has become the tail end of foreign dumping. In addition, years of disasters have arrived, and agricultural production has been poor. Large quantities of people's food rely on foreign imports, resulting in a sharp decline in exports and a sharp increase in imports. The import surplus figures have become even larger. Turning through the customs trade records for the past six years, we know that the import surplus in 1929 was only more than 390 million yuan. By 1930, it suddenly increased to more than 647 million yuan. By 1931, it increased even more sharply to more than 818 million yuan, an increase of more than twice that of the previous eight years. In 1932, due to the large-scale import of foreign rice and wheat, the import surplus figures soared even higher, creating a record of more than 866 million yuan. Although there was a slight decrease in 1933, the number was still as high as more than 733 million yuan. Last year, due to the extreme weakness of domestic consumption and the continued decline in the exchange rate of foreign currencies, both imports and exports declined. The total amount of foreign trade was 1,564,897,503 yuan, of which imports amounted to 1,029,665,224 yuan and exports amounted to 535,214,279 yuan. After offsetting the imports and exports, the annual import surplus was 494,450,945 yuan. As for the trade situation in the first quarter of this year, from January to April, the total amount of foreign trade was 535,155,245 yuan, of which the net value of imports was 357,796,813 yuan and the net value of exports was 177,358,432 yuan. After offsetting the imports and exports, the import surplus was 180,438,381 yuan. The trade deficit for the past six years is unknown in the thousands of billions. The continued continuation of this trade reversal is the greatest underlying cause of the huge outflow of silver. If we do not seek remedies urgently, the day when domestic silver is exhausted will be the time when the entire people's economy goes bankrupt. Thinking about the future of the country, how can we not be terrified? The only ways to balance international trade are to increase exports and reduce imports. Since our country is backward in production and silver prices are high, we cannot imitate other countries and implement foreign dumping. Therefore, in addition to encouraging exporters to export local products as much as possible within a possible range, the only way to offset the trade deficit is to reduce the number of imports of goods. A detailed examination of my country's imports last year shows that cotton textiles, miscellaneous grains, oil candles, machinery, and metals were the largest. Transportation equipment, sugar, tobacco, chemical products, dyes, and pigments were the second largest. The import situation in the first quarter of this year is roughly the same, with rice ranking first, followed by hardware, followed by machine tools, wheat, cotton, wood, dyes and pigments, chemical products, sugar, paper, transportation equipment, cotton cloth, kerosene, and gasoline. Among them, in addition to productive products such as machinery and transportation equipment, the remaining types of imported goods can either be sought domestically, or their quantity can be reduced, or their import can be prohibited. There is room for flexibility in the amount of imports. All countries in the world have already implemented controls on import trade. Moreover, as the country is backward in production and not as good as others in everything, there is even more need to manage it. However, controlling import trade is not only related to the country's economic structure, but also involves foreign trade relations. It cannot be implemented immediately unless the government comes forward to preside over it. The Association is the highest leading body of the entire Shanghai industrial and commercial sector. It should take the interests of the country as the premise and suggest that the government authorities specially establish an import and export trade control agency, or order other competent authorities to select appropriate control methods to implement the management of import and export trade. At the same time, in order to strengthen the power of control, the Central Bank should be authorized to manage international exchange rates and stabilize foreign exchange rates, so as to prevent the outflow of domestic capital, avoid the dumping of exchange rates by various countries, so that the endangered national foundation will not suffer more harm, and the national industry may gradually develop. Benefiting the country and the people are all supported by this. Is this appropriate? I respectfully await your decision."

The Directorate General of Telecommunications Notifies Free Inquiries about Ambiguous Telegrams Relief for Telegram Errors 122

The Shanghai Telegraph Bureau received a letter from the Department of Transportation and Communications stating: "When the recipient of a telegram has doubts about the telegram or believes that there is an error, they should, according to regulations, inquire with the receiving bureau. If there is no error on the part of the receiving bureau, they may use a public telegram to inquire with the sending bureau and notify the recipient of the result. This method was originally set up to provide relief for telegram errors. However, in fact, recipients often do not know how to use this method, or allow the error to stand, and are deeply dissatisfied afterwards, or directly send a telegram to the sender to inquire. If it is found that the error was made by the telegraph bureau, they will request a refund of the round-trip inquiry fees. After the telegraph bureau refuses according to regulations, misunderstandings arise again. Both of the above situations have a significant impact on business reputation. In order to improve the situation, the following two measures are now established: (1) Bureaus with business inspectors should have these inspectors explain the benefits of free telegram inquiries to each sending and receiving user at any time, so that telegram efficiency can be fully realized and business reputation can be increased. (2) If receiving operators in each bureau encounter a recipient who does not understand how to inquire about ambiguous characters and directly sends a telegram to the sender to inquire, or if the sender receives a telegram from the recipient and directly sends a telegram to reply, they should tactfully inform them of the detailed method of inquiring with the telegraph bureau for free, without having to send a telegram themselves, so as to avoid requesting a refund afterwards and causing misunderstandings. Please follow these instructions."

Gale and Heavy Rain in the City Yesterday Morning; Cotton and Rice Flourish, Grain Prices Expected to Drop 127

Since the city received 0.63 inches of rain on the 16th and another 1.2 inches of rain on the 19th, from 8:00 PM on the 21st to the morning of the 22nd, due to the arrival of the Summer Solstice, there was continuous heavy rain, totaling 1.97 inches. From then on, the fields have had sufficient sunshine and water, and the cotton and rice in the suburbs have recovered, temporarily alleviating concerns about a severe drought. China National Aviation Corporation's Shanghai-Guangdong and Shanghai-Beijing flights were suspended due to heavy rain. Details are as follows:

Gale and Rain Last Night

After 5:00 PM yesterday afternoon, the city was again drizzled with light rain. As time went on, the rain became heavier. After 12:00 AM, there were strong winds and heavy rain, and the streets were flooded with several inches of water. The rain gradually stopped at 8:00 AM yesterday morning. It is estimated that from 12:15 AM last night to 9:00 AM yesterday morning, there was a total rainfall of 50.5 millimeters, which is equivalent to 1.97 inches.

Flooding in Low-Lying Areas

Yesterday morning, a reporter from Huadong News Agency took a car to inspect the streets of the city. According to observations, the following low-lying areas were flooded with several inches of water, even up to knee-level in some places: Nanshi, from the roads behind the station, Puyudong Road, Guohuo Road, Difangting, Ximen Road, French Concession Malong Road, Ximen Road, Luban Road, Bobei Road, Sapo Sai Road, Maishen Erdi Luo Road, Public Concession Zhejiang Road, the vicinity of Wing On Company, the vicinity of the Sun Temple in Zhabei, Menghua Street, Cao Ci Lane, Ninghe Road, Qiaojia Zha, and Meijia Nong in the city center. Looking from a high place, they became a waterlogged area. By yesterday morning, the water had gradually receded in the concession areas, but had not completely receded in the city center and Zhabei.

Farmers' Speculation

Checking the seasonal timing, yesterday happened to be the Summer Solstice. Farmers speculate about the weather, saying, "If the southwest wind doesn't bring rain on the Summer Solstice, there will be few bridges," meaning that if there is rain with a westerly wind today, there will be plenty of rain this year. However, it is said that yesterday's rain was entirely caused by a low-pressure system from Jiangxi. Currently, it is an easterly wind, and if it turns to a westerly wind, it may clear up. Yesterday morning, the water level of the Huangpu River was 0.12 feet 4 inches at 8:00 AM, which is lower than the 13.2 feet on the 20th. This tide level needs to be reduced by 1.73 feet according to the Public Works Bureau's baseline.

Flights Suspended

The continuous rainy and foggy weather in this city has inevitably affected transportation. The Shanghai-Guangdong southbound flight of China National Aviation Corporation was not able to fly the day before yesterday due to weather conditions and was postponed to yesterday morning. However, due to the adverse weather, it was still unable to depart. The Shanghai-Beijing northbound flight was also affected by the weather yesterday morning and remained at Longhua Airport. It did not fly out in the afternoon. The Shanghai-Hankou westbound flight was delayed until 8:10 AM yesterday morning before departing from Shanghai.

Grain Prices Fall

After three heavy rains, this city has received 3.8 inches of rain. Therefore, the cotton and rice in the suburbs can fully recover because of this. According to market news, rice crops in various counties of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, and Jiangxi provinces have recovered in recent days, and a good autumn harvest can be expected. Yesterday, the price of rice fell by more than 2 dimes, with the highest price only around 12.5 yuan. The price of wheat was 3.4 yuan, and the price of flour was only 2.512 yuan. It is expected that prices will continue to fall in the coming days.

Rong Zongjing Talks About the Xinkangzhuang Lawsuit 129

According to Central News Agency, Rong Zongjing, a magnate in China's cotton yarn and flour industry, mortgaged a warehouse receipt from Shenxin Third Cotton Mill in Wuxi to Xinkangzhuang (which went bankrupt on February 6 this year) in this city for 60,000 yuan and signed a mortgage contract. When the term expired, Rong had no funds to repay, so the principal sent a letter to Shenxin Third Cotton Mill in Wuxi according to the agreed terms, instructing them to hand over 400 bales of cotton yarn specified on the pledged warehouse receipt as collateral. Subsequently, the mill replied, requesting to continue contacting the original handler. Xinkangzhuang then filed a lawsuit with the Criminal Division of the First Special District Court in the name of shareholder Sun Bosheng, accusing Rong of fraud. The court hearing was held the day before yesterday. Rong did not attend, and the hearing was postponed to the afternoon of the 28th of this month. However, according to Rong, who spoke to the Central News Agency reporter, he has been doing business with Xinkangzhuang for more than 20 years and is also one of its shareholders (Xinkangzhuang has a capital of 300,000 yuan, of which Rong accounts for 60,000 yuan). Due to the failure to receive interest and principal over the years, the total has reached more than 200,000 yuan. Rong originally had 100,000 yuan in business dealings with the bank, which was purely a credit loan. At the end of the year before last, he repaid 41,000 yuan. On the eve of the abolished lunar New Year's Eve (ie, February 2), the paper was used as a guarantee and immediately handed over to the bank by Shenxin's accounting department (however, the warehouse receipt was not signed by Shenxin's general manager (ie, Rong)). Unexpectedly, Xinkangzhuang went bankrupt on February 6. The bank once contacted Rong to repay the loan, and Rong agreed to repay it in installments. Unexpectedly, Sun Bosheng suddenly filed a criminal fraud lawsuit. The reason why Shenxin Third Cotton Mill replied to the bank, requesting to contact the original handler, was because the headquarters did not notify the mills of various matters. Rong continued, stating that the reason why he did not appear in court the day before yesterday was because the plaintiff had expressed a willingness to settle and instructed him not to appear in court. Moreover, the plaintiff also said that he would no longer appear in court, which was actually a deception. Currently, Rong has hired lawyer Guo Shouyi to file a defense with the Special District Court, fundamentally requesting the dismissal of the plaintiff's fraud lawsuit. As for the issue of repaying the loan, it will be discussed after the lawsuit is over.

Someone Threw a Bomb at the Home of Famous Doctor Ding Jiwan; Six Letters Demanding Extortion of 50,000 Yuan; One Bandit Arrested While Arranging a Meeting 130

Ding Jiwan, a descendant of the late famous doctor Ding Ganren, inherited his father's practice at No. 32, Lane 60, Baker Road, and his life was quite prosperous, attracting the attention of bandits. Since last month, he has been receiving threatening letters demanding 50,000 yuan. Ding initially ignored them, but the bandits dared to throw a real explosive bomb into his house through a window one evening. Ding's family was playing mahjong in the living room when they suddenly heard a loud explosion in the kitchen. Greatly shocked, they stopped playing mahjong and rushed to the kitchen to investigate. They saw iron fragments of the bomb scattered on the ground, the glass on the window was shattered, and the walls around the window were also covered with cracks, indicating the intensity of the bomb's explosive power. Fortunately, it was late at night, and the cook and kitchen maids had finished their work and were not in the kitchen, so no one was injured. However, after this incident, Ding became cautious and took the bomb fragments and the threatening letters he had received in recent days to the police station for investigation and requested an investigation. After throwing the bomb, the bandits thought that Ding might soften and continued to send letters to Ding demanding extortion. Ding used a ruse and pretended to agree to meet at 6:30 PM yesterday evening near the Guanghua Grand Theater on Edouard Road. Otherwise, he would report to the police station. The police chief sent detectives Ma Zhongrong and Ye Yushan disguised as vendors to the agreed location. At the appointed time, Ding sent his accountant Xiao Quan disguised to the location. As expected, a bandit named Xia Qingyuan came forward and was arrested by the disguised detectives Ma and Ye. He confessed that another accomplice, Li Sheng (also known as Wu Yongxing, nicknamed "Little Dongyang"), was hiding in Room 34 of the Huxi Hotel on Carter Road. The detectives then went to the address and arrested Wang. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the First Special District Local Court. The police lawyer Qian Xunjiu prosecuted them for extortion under Article 370, Section 1 of the Criminal Law and Article 1, Section 2 of the Regulations for the Punishment of Bandits and explained the process of solving the case. The victim Ding Jiwan and his accountant Xiao Liquan went to court to clarify that they had received a total of six threatening letters and that the walls and windows were damaged by the bomb thrown by the bandits the night before. Judge Liu Yugui questioned Xia and Wang, and they confessed that they were formerly electricians and had the skills to make bombs. The bomb they threw was made by them, and the raw materials were purchased from pharmacies. However, the two bandits did not admit to writing the threatening letters. The court decided that the case required further investigation and ordered the defendants to be detained pending verification of the handwriting of the threatening letters before further trial.

Tianjin Major Fraud Case; Another Criminal Arrested in Shanghai; Fraudulently Obtained a Large Sum of Money from Chinese Merchants Under the Pretense of Releasing Gold from Warehouses 131

The Russian, Po Laiwen, and his accomplices recently defrauded a large sum of money from Xu County in Tianjin. Po has already been arrested by the Tianjin authorities, and his accomplices fled to Shanghai. On the 20th of this month, the Public Concession General Inspectorate sent detectives to arrest the accomplices in the case, the Russian, Xi Huashi Ji, and the Russian woman, Ri Sha Huasha Wen. They were sent to the First Special District Local Court for questioning and detention. It is understood that the criminals in Tianjin used the excuse of investing in Russian gold to swindle the money from the Chinese merchants in Tianjin who were engaged in the sale of gold, collected the gold, and smuggled it elsewhere. The Russians then took the opportunity to sell Russian gold to the buyers. In fact, the Soviet Union strictly prohibits the outflow of gold. Even the small amount of gold needed for dental fillings must be applied for to the government for sale. How could their citizens be allowed to freely export large amounts of gold? The Chinese merchants who were selling gold only knew how to make profits and did not bother to consider the situation, so they fell for Po Laiwen's fraud. At that time, the Russian initially handed over a gold bar to the buyer for testing, and it was deemed to be of the appropriate fineness. After agreeing on the price, the Russians delivered a large number of gold bars, as many as thirty or fifty, to the buyer's location, and the test process was still satisfactory. Therefore, the transaction was completed. Unexpectedly, in that instant, the Russians quickly replaced the real gold with counterfeit gold and fled with the obtained gold price of 50,000 yuan in cash and 31,000 taels of silver in checks. When the buyer discovered that all the gold they had purchased was fake, they quickly reported it to the authorities. Po Laiwen was first found. According to his confession, his accomplices had all left Tianjin and fled to Shanghai. The Public Concession police station urgently telegraphed this city and subsequently arrested the two men and women. At 8:00 AM the day before yesterday, another person, Fu Kesi, was arrested by Xitan at No. 31, Taishan Lane, Shengmu Yuan Road. Fu is the brother-in-law of the Russian woman who was arrested a few days ago and is also heavily involved in the fraud case. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the First Special Court. Judge Ping Shide brought him in for interrogation. The police lawyer Zhang Tianyin briefly described the case and then requested an extension to jointly investigate with Xi Huashi Ji and others. Judge Ma questioned the defendant and ordered the defendant to pay a 3,000 yuan security deposit and change the case to a joint review.

Pusan Town Merchants Plan to Fill in Xuehua Creek 132

Xuehua Creek in Pusan Town (also known as Beixinjing Town) in western Shanghai was originally a river channel that was more than a hundred feet long, located in the center of the town and running east-west. Recently, due to years of disrepair, it has become increasingly silted up, causing garbage to fill it up and emitting a foul odor that makes people want to vomit. Although the merchants in the town have dredged it themselves, it has still become silted up. Now that summer has arrived, it poses a significant health hazard. Because the creek does not have an important position, only due to water discharge problems, the merchants have repeatedly discussed and decided to fill in the river channel and build a large culvert underneath for water discharge. The necessary expenses will be covered by the sale of the filled-in land, which can also be used to widen the streets in the future. It is truly a win-win situation. They are currently working on the plan and will implement it soon.
